</th>
<td>3 sections
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Composition Year
</th>
<td>1850, 1853–54
</td></tr>

</th>

<h2> <span class="mw-headline" id="Misc._Comments">Misc. Comments</span></h2>
<h4> <span class="mw-headline" id="Publication_History">Publication History</span></h4>
<ul><li>Paris: 1852 (<i>La fuite en Égypte</i> only, full score)
</li><li>Paris: 1855, Œuvre 25 (full score)
</li><li>Leipzig: Breitkopf und Härtel, n.d. (1901), as part of Hector Berlioz Werke (1900–07), Serie IV, Band IX, edited by Charles Malherbe and Felix Weingartner; overture to <i>La Fuite en Égypte</i> published separately in Serie II, Band V (1901) 
</li><li>Kassel: Bärenreiter, 1998, BA 5451, as part of New Berlioz Edition (1967–2005), Volume 11, edited by David Lloyd-Jones
</li></ul>
